The\\n1606:         return value depends on the value of result_type.\\n1607: \\n1608:         When result_type is:\\n1609:         - MULTI: Retrieves all rows using fetchmany(). Wraps in an iterator for\\n1610:            chunked reads when supported.\\n1611:         - SINGLE: Retrieves a single row using fetchone().\\n1612:         - ROW_COUNT: Retrieves the number of rows in the result.\\n1613:         - CURSOR: Runs the query, and returns the cursor object. It is the\\n1614:            caller's responsibility to close the cursor.\\n1615:         \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n1616:         result_type = result_type or NO_RESULTS\\n1617:         try:\\n1618:             sql, params = self.as_sql()\\n1619:             if not sql:\\n1620:                 raise EmptyResultSet\\n1621:         except EmptyResultSet:\\n1622:             if result_type == MULTI:\\n1623:                 return iter([])\\n1624:             else:\\n1625:                 return\\n1626:         if chunked_fetch:\\n1627:             cursor = self.connection.chunked_cursor()\\n1628:         else:\\n1629:             cursor = self.connection.cursor()\\n1630:         try:\\n1631:             cursor.execute(sql, params)\\n1632:         except Exception as e:\\n1633:             # done with the cursor\\n1656:                 cursor.close()\\n1657:         if result_type == NO_RESULTS:\\n1658:             cursor.close()\\n1659:             return\\n1660: \\n1661:         result = cursor_iter(\\n1662:             cursor,\\n1663:             self.connection.features.empty_fetchmany_value,\\n1664:             self.col_count if self.has_extra_select else None,\\n1665:             chunk_size,\\n1666:         )\\n1667:         if not chunked_fetch or not self.connection.features.can_use_chunked_reads:\\n1668:             #
